#{{{ Setup timer after ladder has disappeared. Called from T5381h only.
SetupDisappearingLadderTimer:
TA7A4h	3A07EC..  :...	LD	A,(TEC07H)		; A = 0xEC07
;; TA7BEh jumps conditionally to here.
TA7A7h	B7......  ....	OR	A			; Set flags
TA7A8h	C8......  ....	RET	Z			; if (A==0) return

; 0xEC07 != 0. This means ladder has disappeared.
TA7A9h	3A00EC..  :...	LD	A,(TEC00H)		; A = number/id/index of disappearing ladder
TA7ACh	87......  ....	ADD	A,A			; A += A (since struct is 2 bytes)
TA7ADh	4F......  O...	LD	C,A			; C = A
TA7AEh	0600....  ....	LD	B,000h			; BC = A
TA7B0h	21AEE0..  !...	LD	HL,0E0AEh		; HL = 0xE0AE, start of disappearing ladder timers. Actual start is at 0xe0B0
TA7B3h	09......  ....	ADD	HL,BC			; HL += BC, go to wanted index
TA7B4h	3602....  6...	LD	(HL),002h		; Set state to: timer is still counting down?
TA7B6h	2C......  ,...	INC	L			; Point HL to "reappear timer".
TA7B7h	363C....  6<..	LD	(HL),03Ch		; Set reappear disappeared timer to 0x3c ticks.
TA7B9h	AF......  ....	XOR	A			; Clear A and F
TA7BAh	3200EC..  2...	LD	(TEC00H),A		; Clear ID/number/index of disappearing ladder.
TA7BDh	C9......  ....	RET			
# }}}
